What Leceister city football club has produced in the last 5-6 years has been just simply magnificent. If any team deserves a documentary series, it has got to be Leicester City FC.  From winning the 5000/1 title, the story of Jamie Vardy's rise. Selling players like Mahrez, Maguire, Kante and yet still having a team capable of challenging in Europe. Losing their team owner in a devastating crash, that happened next to the football, and yet their resilience showed by the whole Leicester team from the top to the bottom, has been truly wonderful. What his son carried on from his dad on building this football club and connecting with the fans around, has to be something every other football club ( mainly the so-called top 6) should be jealous of. Even the work Brendan Rodgers has done to this team, as much as I enjoyed Liverpool's collapse during their title race in 2014, I am happy for him, went away to Scotland, increased his stock price, came back to England, took over a solid team, and made it more consistent. Although they fell off last season from the UCL spot, I do hope they do play in UCL next season. Even big shout out to Hamza Choudhary for representing south Asians and being the first player of that descent to win the FA Cup <3  Overall, Leceister city made us all love football again, and they continue to show us what proper ownership can do for a football club.
